❯ 404 error not found                                                           

⏺ A 404 usually means the app can't find the data. Let me help you check:

  Most likely cause: The Supabase database schema wasn't run yet.

  To fix this:
  1. Go to your https://supabase.com/dashboard
  2. Select your project
  3. Go to SQL Editor (left sidebar)
  4. Copy and paste the contents of pms/supabase-schema.sql and run it

  This creates the users and daily_entries tables.

  Also verify in Vercel:
  1. Go to your Vercel project dashboard
  2. Click Settings → Environment Variables
  3. Make sure these are set:
    - NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL
    - NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY
    - SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY
    - PMS_PASSWORD

  Did you run the schema in Supabase? Let me know what you see.

  - Name it pms

  Step 2: Push code to GitHub
  cd /Users/anishpatel/Documents/Projects/pms
  git remote add origin https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/pms.git
  git branch -M main
  git push -u origin main

  Step 3: Deploy on Vercel
  - Go to https://vercel.com → New Project
  - Import your pms GitHub repo
  - Root Directory: pms (if needed)

  ┌───────────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────┐

  │ PMS_PASSWORD                  │ 0000                           │
  └───────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────┘

  - Click Deploy

  Step 4: Run the database schema

❯ remote: Invalid username or token. Password authentication is not supported   
for Git operations.                                                             
fatal: Authentication failed for 'https://github.com/apatel26/pms1.git/'        

⏺ You need a GitHub Personal Access Token to push code. Here's how to fix it:

  Step 1: Create a GitHub token
  1. Go to https://github.com/settings/tokens
  2. Click Generate new token (classic)
  3. Name it "PMS Deploy"
  4. Check repo scope (full control)
  5. Click Generate token and copy it

  Step 2: Push with token
  Instead of your password, use the token when prompted:

  git push -u origin main

  When it asks for password, paste your GitHub token (not your actual password).

  ---
  If you want to avoid entering the token each time, you can store it:

  git config --global credential.helper store

  Then push once with the token and it will be saved.

  ---
  Do you already have a GitHub token set up? Or do you need to create one?

❯ remote: Repository not found.                                                 
fatal: repository 'https://github.com/apatel26/pms1.git/' not found             
⏺ The repo pms1 was deleted (you said you were going to clean slate). You need
  to create a new repo on GitHub first.

  Step 1: Create new repo on GitHub
  - Go to https://github.com/new
  - Name it pms (or pms-app)
  - Don't check "Initialize with README"
  - Click Create repository

  Step 2: Update the remote and push
  git remote set-url origin https://github.com/apatel26/pms.git
  git push -u origin main

  (Replace apatel26 with your GitHub username and pms with whatever name you
  gave the repo)

  Let me know once you've created the GitHub repo and what you named it.

⏺ Code is pushed to GitHub. Now let's deploy on Vercel.

  Step 3: Deploy on Vercel

  1. Go to https://vercel.com
  2. Click Add New → Project
  3. Find your pms repo and click Import
  4. Under Root Directory, make sure it says pms (if not, click Edit and set it)
  5. Click Environment Variables and add these 4:

  ┌───────────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐
  │             Name              │              Value               │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL      │ (your Supabase URL)              │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY │ (your Supabase anon key)         │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY     │ (your Supabase service role key) │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ PMS_PASSWORD                  │ 0000                             │
  └───────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────┘

  6. Click Deploy

  Once deployed, let me know the URL and we can test it together.

⏺ When importing in Vercel, for the Project Name, use only letters, digits, and
  underscores (no dashes).

  Use something like:
  - pms_app
  - pms_hotel
  - hotel_pms

  Or just pms if that's available.

  Make sure the Project Name field looks like: pms (no spaces, no dashes)

❯ how do I open on safari                                                       

⏺ To open Console in Safari:

  1. Go to Safari → Settings (or Preferences)
  2. Click the Advanced tab
  3. Check the box "Show Develop menu in menu bar"
  4. Close Settings
  5. Now go to Develop → Show JavaScript Console

  Or press Option + Command + C

  To deploy:
  1. Go to Vercel

  3. Add environment variables
  4. Deploy

  What's included in Phase 1:
  - Modern dark UI with amber/gold accents
  - Login page with "American Inn and RV Park" branding
  - Daily Entry page with grid view for rooms and RV sites
  - Add Entry modal with:
    - Guest Rooms (101-212) and RV Sites (1-15)
    - Standard rate ($70) or custom rate
    - Pet fees ($20/night default or custom)
    - Extra charges
    - Cash/CC payment
    - Refund option
    - Backdate support
  - Reports page with monthly/weekly/daily views
  - Excel and PDF export
  - Settings page (property info, tax rates, RV rates)
  - Yearly reset and factory reset buttons (placeholder)

  Still need to do (Phase 2):
  - Housekeeping module
  - Custom roles system
  - Audit log
  - Cloud backup integration
  - Photo upload
